# Wiki Log

> 所有 wiki 操作的按时间顺序记录。只追加，不修改。
> 格式：`## [YYYY-MM-DD] action | subject`
> Actions: ingest, update, query, lint, create, archive, delete
> 当此文件超过 500 条时，轮换：重命名为 log-YYYY.md，重新开始。

  2. **feat — Hindsight observation_scopes 可配置 `a376ca008`**：`plugins/memory/hindsight/__init__.py:21` 文档 `HINDSIGHT_RETAIN_OBSERVATION_SCOPES` env + `:330 _load_config` 读 + `:381 _OBSERVATION_SCOPE_KEYWORDS={"per_tag","combined","all_combinations"}` + `:384 _normalize_observation_scopes()` 接受 keyword/JSON list-of-lists/扁平 tag list + `:1240-1243/:1498-1499` retain kwargs 注入 + `:1614-1620` **tool retain 路径切** `client.aretain → client.aretain_batch` 因前者不接此参
  3. **feat — `/status` 显 model+context `ead38107a`**：`gateway/slash_commands.py:395-509 _handle_status_command()` 优先 live `status_agent` (model/provider/context_compressor.last_prompt_tokens/.context_length) → SessionDB row → user config + 新 locale 键 `gateway.status.model/model_provider/context/context_used` + 17 locale 同步 + 73 行测试
  4. **feat — Display 显 `delegate_task` goals `5035fa902`**：`agent/display.py:180 _delegate_task_goal_parts` + `:212-222 build_tool_preview` 渲 `"{count} tasks: Goal A | Goal B | Goal C"` 批量 + `:1057-1060 _get_cute_tool_message_impl` 渲 `"3x: Goal A | Goal B"`
  5. **Auth — xAI OAuth 跨 profile 解析 + write-through global root + access skew 120→3600s（PR #43589 salvage 5 commit）**：`f1d6f0436 hermes_cli/auth.py:3899 _xai_oauth_state_from_store()` 扫 `credential_pool["xai-oauth"]` + `:3937 _xai_oauth_state_has_usable_tokens()` 守 + `:3946-3956 _read_xai_oauth_tokens()` profile 缺 → global root；`497352bc4 :1087 _save_auth_store` 加 `target_path` 参 + `:3996 _profile_has_own_xai_oauth_state()` + `:4007 _write_through_xai_oauth_to_global_root()` 含 **pytest 安全带 `:4030`** + `:4061-4079 _save_xai_oauth_tokens` write-through 在 `_auth_store_lock()` 内；`febdddb41 :111 XAI_ACCESS_TOKEN_REFRESH_SKEW_SECONDS=3600`（原 120）适配 6h xAI access token；`1227007ae scripts/release.py:1557` AUTHOR_MAP `andrewdmwalker@gmail.com=capt-marbles`；`8844e091c` merge
  6. **MCP — fail-fast noninteractive OAuth `dcc321695`**：`tools/mcp_oauth.py:756-763 build_oauth_auth()` 现 `raise OAuthNonInteractiveError(...)` 在 `not _is_interactive() and not storage.has_cached_tokens()` 时，消息含 `hermes mcp login {server_name}` hint + `tools/mcp_oauth_manager.py:411/427-434 MCPOAuthManager` 镜像 + `tools/mcp_tool.py:2165` 已捕作可恢复 skip
  7. **Disk-cleanup protected walks 显式 frozenset + 后序 DFS（`c1a70a543/40699c329/a688d2a1b`）**：`plugins/disk-cleanup/disk_cleanup.py:147 _EMPTY_DIR_PROTECTED_TOP_LEVEL` 14 项 + `:153 _EMPTY_DIR_SWEEP_PRUNE_DIRS={".git","node_modules","venv",".venv","site-packages","__pycache__"}` + `:364-402 quick()` 空目录 sweep 重写 `sweep_stack: List[Tuple[Path, bool]]` 显式后序 DFS（替 `hermes_home.rglob("*")` 全遍历防 gateway event loop 卡分钟级）+ `visited` bool 后序标记 + 测 `tests/plugins/test_disk_cleanup_plugin.py +12`
  8. **API debug dump 全字段 redact + Notion `ntn_` 模式（`ad58dd51a + aab2e99ba`）**：`agent/agent_runtime_helpers.py:1228-1231 dump_api_request_debug()` 经 `redact_sensitive_text(serialized, force=True)` + `atomic_json_write(dump_file, _redacted_payload, default=str)` + `:1236 HERMES_DUMP_REQUEST_STDOUT` 也走 redacted；`agent/redact.py:107 _PREFIX_PATTERNS` 加 `r"ntn_[A-Za-z0-9]{10,}"`（Notion internal integration token）；dump 现**无条件**在 API 错误时落
  9. **Gateway scoped lock 第三 stale 分支 `ec05d2bc3`**：`gateway/status.py:646-660 acquire_scoped_lock()` 新分支：PID + start_time 都非 None 且相等但 `not _looks_like_gateway_process(existing_pid)` 时调 `_read_process_cmdline` 检 cmdline 可读 → `stale=True`，防 Linux/systemd 启动期 PID+jiffy 重用让 cron/nginx/sshd 冒名 gateway；保守：cmdline 不可读不 evict
  10. **Bedrock `boto3>=1.34.59` 软守 `2cddc9c89`**：`agent/bedrock_adapter.py:61 _MIN_BOTO3_VERSION=(1,34,59)` + `:64-88 _require_boto3()` 解析 `boto3.__version__` 三 int tuple；低版 `RuntimeError` 含升级 hint；parse 失败不阻塞 — 修 Ubuntu 24.04 系统 `boto3==1.34.46` shadow venv pin 致 `converse_stream` 裸 `AttributeError`
  11. **s6 / Supervisor 5 修硬化**：`40d7c264f #46266` `register_profile_gateway(start_now=False)` + `(tmp_dir/"down").touch()` marker；`61ee2dbfd #46291` `service_manager.py:756 _render_log_run` 加 logs gateways 父目录 chown + `docker/stage2-hook.sh:319` cont-init 预创父；`b77096726 #46292` `:359 _write_gateway_desired_state(name, desired_state)` + `container_boot.py:258 _read_desired_state` 优先 `desired_state` 字段防 transient 抹运维意图；`c2b7669ad #46289` `:758 rm -f "$log_dir/lock"` 在 chown 后 s6-log exec 前清陈旧 lockfile；`95715dcb0 #46483` `hermes_cli/main.py:467 _apply_profile_override` 守 `if profile_name is None and not os.environ.get("HERMES_S6_SUPERVISED_CHILD")` 让 supervised `gateway-default` 跳过 sticky `active_profile`
  12. **Container / Dashboard 4 修**：`4eb0ff639 #46290` `service_manager.py:118` gate 改为裸 `_s6_running()` 修 Fly Firecracker microVM；`aca11c227 #46293` `_is_dashboard_container()` autodetect 跳 reconcile；`80f8ffc74 #46487` machine-dashboard reroute 钉 `get_default_hermes_root()` 防 `$HOME/.hermes` fallback；`f79551378 #45120` `scripts/install.ps1:1431-1442` 重建 venv 前 `taskkill /F /T /IM hermes.exe /FI "PID ne $myPid"` + 800ms sleep 释 `_bcrypt.pyd` 锁

  - **Photon 入站/出站附件 + 语音**：`314af28e8 feat(photon): download and inline inbound attachments`：sidecar 端 `sidecar/index.mjs:57-58 MAX_INLINE_ATTACHMENT_BYTES = 20 * 1024 * 1024` env 可覆盖；`normalizeContent()`（`index.mjs:219-230`）拆 text/attachment/voice；`normalizeBinaryContent()`（`:168-217`）调 `content.read()` → `Buffer.from(buf).toString("base64")` 内联 + `meta.encoding = "base64"`；over-cap 只发 metadata；Python 端 `adapter.py _dispatch_inbound()` 新 `media_urls + media_types`，attachment 经新 `_cache_inbound_attachment(content, name, mime)`（`adapter.py:977-1026`）按 mime 路由到 `cache_image_from_bytes / cache_audio_from_bytes / cache_document_from_bytes`，image cache 抛 `ValueError`（HEIC magic）降级到 document cache；新 `_IMAGE_EXT_BY_MIME / _AUDIO_EXT_BY_MIME` mirrors BlueBubbles；text 设短 marker `"(attachment)"` 让 group mention-gating 与普通消息一致；`MessageEvent` 加 `media_urls / media_types`；`dbf2470d4 feat(photon): Add voice message support` underthestars-zhy：`ctype in {"attachment","voice"}`, `is_voice = ctype == "voice"`, `mtype = MessageType.VOICE if is_voice else _attachment_message_type(mime)`，`_cache_inbound_attachment` 新 `force_audio: bool = False` kwarg，扩展名默 `.m4a`；`4615e08d3 feat(photon): wire outbound media via spectrum-ts attachment() (#42397)` Teknium：sidecar `/send-attachment` 端点构 `attachment(path, opts) / voice(path, opts)` builder + `space.send(spectrumText(caption))` 单独 caption；adapter `send_image / send_image_file / send_voice / send_video / send_document / send_animation` 六方法 override；URL 类先 `cache_image_from_url` 落地；`_sidecar_send_attachment` defense-in-depth 调 `BasePlatformAdapter.validate_media_delivery_path(str(path))`；cron `_standalone_send` 多附件支持

  - **TUI cgroup-aware V8 heap cap** (`2f523a469`)：`ui-tui/src/lib/memoryMonitor.ts:20-50 resolveThresholds(criticalBytes?, highBytes?)` 改从 `getHeapStatistics().heap_size_limit` 派生阈值 fallback 8GB ceiling：`critical = Math.max(2*GB, Math.round(ceiling * 0.88))` ~88% / `high = Math.max(1*GB, Math.min(critical - 256*MB, Math.round(ceiling * 0.7)))` ~70%；之前硬编码 2.5GB 在 8GB heap ceiling 下相当于 ~31% 就触发 critical exit 静默关 gateway stdin；`ui-tui/src/entry.tsx:1 #!/usr/bin/env -S node --max-old-space-size=8192 --expose-gc` shebang 钉 ceiling；影响：1GB 容器/cgroup 限制 Docker 里跑 TUI 不再因没到 2.5GB 就静默 OOM
  - **State `PRAGMA wal_checkpoint(TRUNCATE)`** (`46b2afc56` + `19db9cd07`)：`hermes_state.py:597,617-651 _try_wal_checkpoint(self) -> None` Best-effort 永不 raise + 文档"TRUNCATE may block writers briefly while checkpointing, but _try_wal_checkpoint is called off the hot path (every 50..."；commit 路径每 50 次写 off-hot-path 触发；`:651-657` exit/dispose 时 TRUNCATE 让退出进程先收 WAL；`:4107` 显式 checkpoint；长跑进程 `state.db-wal` 不再单调增长；配套 `19db9cd07 fix(acp): replace direct db._lock/_conn access with public update_session_meta()` ACP 不再绕封装让新 WAL 收尾失效
